                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>This volatility may be great for bitcoin investors, but the </span><a href=&quot;https://finance.yahoo.com/news/bitcoin-needs-become-real-currency-134831445.html&quot;><span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>growth has hindered bitcoin’s effectiveness as a currency</span></a><span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>, as people are reluctant to spend or transact during a surge.                       </div>

                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>In 2014 Overstock (</span><a href=&quot;https://finance.yahoo.com/quote/OSTK?ltr=1&quot;><span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>OSTK</span></a><span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>) was the first major retailer to accept bitcoin, becoming the first billion-dollar business to take the leap. The company’s strategy was to pocket 10% of a sale in bitcoin and convert the rest into U.S. dollars. To facilitate transactions, Overstock used Coinbase’s exchange to convert digital currency in real-time.</span>" data-reactid="41"><span style="font-weight:400;">In 2014 Overstock (</span><a href="https://finance.yahoo.com/quote/OSTK?ltr=1"><span style="font-weight:400;">OSTK</span></a><span style="font-weight:400;">) was the first major retailer to accept bitcoin, becoming the first billion-dollar business to take the leap. The company’s strategy was to pocket 10% of a sale in bitcoin and convert the rest into U.S. dollars. To facilitate transactions, Overstock used Coinbase’s exchange to convert digital currency in real-time.</span></p>
                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>But during the surge this year, Overstock CEO Patrick Byrne changed the online retailer’s policy in two major ways.</span>" data-reactid="42"><span style="font-weight:400;">But during the surge this year, Overstock CEO Patrick Byrne changed the online retailer’s policy in two major ways.</span></p>
                   <h2 class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<b>Overstock’s new policy: keep half</b>" data-reactid="43"><b>Overstock’s new policy: keep half</b></h2>
                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>“What we do now is 50% gets turned into U.S. dollars and 50% gets held as bitcoin,” Byrne told Yahoo Finance. “So we’re accumulating that bitcoin.”</span>" data-reactid="44"><span style="font-weight:400;">“What we do now is 50% gets turned into U.S. dollars and 50% gets held as bitcoin,” Byrne told Yahoo Finance. “So we’re accumulating that bitcoin.”</span></p>
                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="In the first week of August, Overstock announced it would be accepting nearly all major cryptocurrencies by partnering with ShapeShift, another exchange. However, alternate cryptocurrencies that the company will retain on its books will be converted into bitcoin." data-reactid="45">In the first week of August, Overstock announced it would be accepting nearly all major cryptocurrencies by partnering with ShapeShift, another exchange. However, alternate cryptocurrencies that the company will retain on its books will be converted into bitcoin.</p>
                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>Beyond holding, Byrne said the company doesn’t use any swaps or forwards or any other fancy financial instruments to hedge Overstock’s bitcoin investments.</span>" data-reactid="46"><span style="font-weight:400;">Beyond holding, Byrne said the company doesn’t use any swaps or forwards or any other fancy financial instruments to hedge Overstock’s bitcoin investments.</span></p>
                   <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>“Just by accumulating half, that just feels like the right number for now,” Byrne said. In his view, the risk doesn’t lie as much in bitcoin but in government currency.</span>" data-reactid="47"><span style="font-weight:400;">“Just by accumulating half, that just feels like the right number for now,” Byrne said. In his view, the risk doesn’t lie as much in bitcoin but in government currency.</span></p>

But in reality, it’s not much: just about one-sixth of 1% &nbsp;(0.15% to be precise). Even if it is, however, Byrne’s policy probably won’t change.</span></p>
                    <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>“I think people should think about hedging risk in fiat currency,” he said. “It’s just what some government mandarin created with a pen. Why don’t they hedge risk in holding that? The risk isn’t bitcoin to the dollar. The question is why are we doing business in dollars when we could do it in bitcoin?”</span>" data-reactid="64"><span style="font-weight:400;">“I think people should think about hedging risk in fiat currency,” he said. “It’s just what some government mandarin created with a pen.                     <h2 class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<b>Bitcoin still struggles to be a transactional currency</b>" data-reactid="65"><b>Bitcoin still struggles to be a transactional currency</b></h2>
                    <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>Byrne laments the investing-over-using mentality that the surge has engendered for the small bitcoin transaction volume on Overstock&amp;nbsp;— though considering most of the population is bitcoin-illiterate, 0.15% may actually be a sizable amount.</span>" data-reactid="66"><span style="font-weight:400;">Byrne laments the investing-over-using mentality that the surge has engendered for the small bitcoin transaction volume on Overstock&nbsp;— though considering most of the population is bitcoin-illiterate, 0.15% may actually be a sizable amount.</span></p>
                    <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>“People just wanna hold onto it rather than spend it — they want to hoard it,” said Byrne. “You know the first bitcoin transaction? The guy who sent it gave 10,000 bitcoins for a pizza. That was a $35 million pizza [today]. So everyone’s a bit afraid to spend.”</span>" data-reactid="67"><span style="font-weight:400;">“People just wanna hold onto it rather than spend it — they want to hoard it,” said Byrne. “You know the first bitcoin transaction? The guy who sent it gave 10,000 bitcoins for a pizza. That was a $35 million pizza [today]. So everyone’s a bit afraid to spend.”</span></p>
                    <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="“When Overstock decided to open its doors to bitcoin, it was charting unknown territory,” said Byrne. &amp;nbsp;“It accelerated the familiarization of the cryptocurrency by years.” Byrne would love if others took a similar leap, even if on a smaller level." data-reactid="68">“When Overstock decided to open its doors to bitcoin, it was charting unknown territory,” said Byrne. &nbsp;“It accelerated the familiarization of the cryptocurrency by years.” Byrne would love if others took a similar leap, even if on a smaller level.</p>
                    <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="“If people would start using it, it would get more liquid, more valuable,” he said. “I wish people who held bitcoin would take 10% and say ‘I am gonna spend this to stimulate the market.’”" data-reactid="69">“If people would start using it, it would get more liquid, more valuable,” he said. “I wish people who held bitcoin would take 10% and say ‘I am gonna spend this to stimulate the market.’”</p>
                    <p class="canvas-atom canvas-text Mb(1.0em) Mb(0)--sm Mt(0.8em)--sm" type="text" content="<span style=&quot;font-weight:400;&quot;>So what’s stimulating the market now? One person in the family might be bragging about success in the recent bitcoin surge and another family member says, “great, now go buy us some new things for the house.”</span>" data-reactid="70"><span style="font-weight:400;">So what’s stimulating the market now? One person in the family might be bragging about success in the recent bitcoin surge and another family member says, “great, now go buy us some new things for the house.”</span></p>
